===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\BusinessObject\BusinessObjectMSKTOBAllashirdetesek.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<BusinessObject xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/businessobject">
	<DataTable>msk_tob_allashirdetesek</DataTable>
	<UniqueIDColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</UniqueIDColumn>
	<Fields>
		<Field name="Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID" />
		<Field name="Idkeresesikerelem">
			<DefaultValue type="Constant" return="int" default="0">[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]</DefaultValue>
		</Field>
		<Field name="Targy" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="StatuszID" />
		<Field name="Datum_lejarat" />
		<Field name="Fejlecszoveg" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Feladatok" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Tulajdonsagok" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Elvarasok" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Elonytjelent" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Juttatasok" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Tovabbi_info" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Toborzo_info" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Toborzonev" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Toborzotelefonszam" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Vallalatibemutatkozo" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Datum_jovahagyas" />
		<Field name="Datum_publikalas" />
		<Field name="Link" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
		<Field name="Datum_lezaras" />
		<Field name="VegzettsegiszintID" />
		<Field name="Pubcsoportportal" />
		<Field name="PubCVO" />
		<Field name="PubSTA" />
		<Field name="FenykepURL" />
		<Field name="VideoURL" />
		<Field name="LetrehozoID">
			<DefaultValue type="Constant" return="int" default="1">'[##Session.UserID##]'</DefaultValue>
		</Field>
	</Fields>
	<Methods>
		<BeforeSave>
			<RunSQL><![CDATA[
					DECLARE @ID_table TABLE(
					ID INT NULL,
					StatuszOLD INT NULL,
					StatuszNEW INT	NULL
					)

					INSERT INTO @ID_table SELECT '[##Field.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID##]', a.StatuszID, '[##Field.StatuszID##]' FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek a
          WHERE a.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = '[##Field.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID##]'

					DECLARE @MailSendLogID INT
					DECLARE @MyCursor CURSOR
					DECLARE @ID INT
					DECLARE @StatuszOLD INT
					DECLARE @StatuszNEW INT
					DECLARE	@CimzettID INT
					DECLARE @CimzettNeve VARCHAR(200)
					DECLARE @CimzettEmail VARCHAR(100)
					DECLARE @Targy VARCHAR(8000)
					DECLARE @Szoveg VARCHAR(8000)
					DECLARE @TemplateID INT
					DECLARE @LetrehozoID INT
					DECLARE @LetrehozoEmail VARCHAR(100)
					DECLARE @LetrehozoNeve VARCHAR(200)
					DECLARE @KKID INT
					DECLARE @KKName VARCHAR(255)
					DECLARE @Idceg INT
					DECLARE @base_url VARCHAR(8000) = (SELECT TOP 1 CodeValue FROM dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup WHERE Code='BaseURL' AND Deleted=0)
					DECLARE @url VARCHAR(8000) = '%base%MMMSKTOBToborzas/ScreenMSKTOBFeladatkosar'
					SET @url = REPLACE(@url, '%base%', ISNULL(@base_url, ''))
					DECLARE @Letrehozo_vallalatID INT	
					DECLARE @Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev VARCHAR(40)
					BEGIN
						SET @MyCursor = CURSOR FOR
						select ID, StatuszOLD, StatuszNEW from @ID_table

							OPEN @MyCursor 
							FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor 
							INTO @ID, @StatuszOLD, @StatuszNEW

							WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
							BEGIN
								/* Email az álláshirdetést engedélyezo részére */
								IF @StatuszNEW = 25 AND @StatuszOLD <> 25
								BEGIN
									SET @LetrehozoID = (SELECT TOP 1 ISNULL(LetrehozoID,1) FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)
									SET @Idceg = (SELECT TOP 1 c.VallalatKod FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek i LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=i.Idkeresesikerelem 
													LEFT JOIN dbo.orn_SZI_Company c ON c.AllasVallalatKod=kk.Idceg
													WHERE i.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)

									SET @Letrehozo_vallalatID = (SELECT TOP 1 CompanyID FROM dbo.orn_SZI_Company WHERE VallalatKod=@Idceg)

									SET @Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev = (SELECT TOP 1 RovidNev FROM dbo.msk_Company WHERE BUKRS=@Idceg)
									SET @TemplateID = (SELECT top 1 EmailTemplateSampleID FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE  technical_name=CONCAT('tob_',@Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev,'_elkuldott') AND Deleted=0 AND CompanyID=@Letrehozo_vallalatID)

									SET @Targy = (SELECT top 1 EmailSubject FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)
									SET @Szoveg = (SELECT top 1 EmailBody FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)

									SET @KKID = (SELECT TOP 1 Idkeresesikerelem FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)
									SET @KKName = (SELECT Cim FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)

									SET @CimzettID = (SELECT TOP 1 Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)
									SET @CimzettEmail = (SELECT TOP 1 Email FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@CimzettID)
									SET @CimzettNeve = (SELECT TOP 1 Name FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID = @CimzettID)

									SET @Targy = REPLACE(@Targy, '%allashirdetes_neve%', @KKName)

									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%cimzett%', ISNULL(@CimzettNeve, 'Címzett'))
									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%link%', ISNULL(@url, ''))
									
									INSERT INTO dbo.msk_MailSend_Log
									(
										Modul,
										Recipients,
										CopyRecipients,
										BlindCopyRecipients,
										Subject,
										Body,
										BodyFormat,
										Importance,
										FileAttachments,
										MailItemID,
										Created,
										Success,
										Deleted,
										EmailTemplateID,
										CreatedBy,
										SentToJelentkezoID,
										SentToJelentkezoTablaID
									)
									VALUES
									(   'TOB',        -- Modul - varchar(50)
										@CimzettEmail,        -- Recipients - varchar(260)
										NULL,        -- CopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
										NULL,        -- BlindCopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
										@Targy,        -- Subject - varchar(200)
										@Szoveg,        -- Body - varchar(max)
										'HTML',        -- BodyFormat - varchar(20)
										'Normal',        -- Importance - varchar(100)
										'',        -- FileAttachments - varchar(8000)
										0,         -- MailItemID - int
										GETDATE(), -- Created - datetime
										0,      -- Success - bit
										0,         -- Deleted - tinyint
										@TemplateID,         -- EmailTemplateID - int
										@LetrehozoID,         -- CreatedBy - int
										@CimzettID,         -- SentToJelentkezoID - int
										0          -- SentToJelentkezoTablaID - tinyint
										)

									SET @MailSendLogID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

									EXEC [dbo].[msk_SendMail_dll] 	
											@Modul = 'TOB',
											@Recipients = @CimzettEmail,
											@CopyRecipients  = '',
											@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
											@Subject = @Targy,
											@Body = @Szoveg,
											@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
											@Importance = 'Normal',
											@FileAttachments = NULL,
											@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
											@CreatedBy = @LetrehozoID,
											@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
											@CimzettTablaID = 0,
											@MailSendLogID = @MailSendLogID

									--exec [dbo].[msk_SendMail]
									--	@Modul = 'TOB',
									--	@Recipients = @CimzettEmail,
									--	@CopyRecipients  = NULL,
									--	@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
									--	@Subject = @Targy,
									--	@Body = @Szoveg,
									--	@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
									--	@Importance = 'Normal',
									--	@FileAttachments = NULL,
									--	@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
									--	@CreatedBy = @LetrehozoID,
									--	@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
									--	@CimzettTablaID = 0
								END

								/* Email az álláshirdetés létrehozójának engedélyezést követoen */
								IF @StatuszNEW = 21 AND @StatuszOLD <> 21
								BEGIN
									SET @LetrehozoID = (SELECT TOP 1 LetrehozoID FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)
									SET @LetrehozoEmail = (SELECT TOP 1 Email FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@LetrehozoID)
									SET @LetrehozoNeve = (SELECT TOP 1 Name FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@LetrehozoID)
									SET @Idceg = (SELECT TOP 1 c.VallalatKod FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek i LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=i.Idkeresesikerelem 
													LEFT JOIN dbo.orn_SZI_Company c ON c.AllasVallalatKod=kk.Idceg
													WHERE i.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)
									SET @Letrehozo_vallalatID = (SELECT TOP 1 CompanyID FROM dbo.orn_SZI_Company WHERE VallalatKod=@Idceg)

									SET @Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev = (SELECT TOP 1 RovidNev FROM dbo.msk_Company WHERE BUKRS=@Idceg)

									SET @TemplateID = (SELECT top 1 EmailTemplateSampleID FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE  technical_name=CONCAT('tob_',@Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev,'_engedelyezett') AND Deleted=0 AND CompanyID=@Letrehozo_vallalatID)
									
									SET @KKID = (SELECT TOP 1 Idkeresesikerelem FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@ID)
									SET @KKName = (SELECT Cim FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)
									
									SET @Targy = (SELECT top 1 EmailSubject FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)
									SET @Targy = REPLACE(@Targy, '%allashirdetes_neve%', @KKName)
									SET @Szoveg = (SELECT top 1 EmailBody FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)
						


									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%cimzett%', ISNULL(@LetrehozoNeve, 'Címzett'))
									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
									SET @Szoveg = REPLACE(@Szoveg, '%link%', ISNULL(@url, ''))

									INSERT INTO dbo.msk_MailSend_Log
									(
										Modul,
										Recipients,
										CopyRecipients,
										BlindCopyRecipients,
										Subject,
										Body,
										BodyFormat,
										Importance,
										FileAttachments,
										MailItemID,
										Created,
										Success,
										Deleted,
										EmailTemplateID,
										CreatedBy,
										SentToJelentkezoID,
										SentToJelentkezoTablaID
									)
									VALUES
									(   'TOB',        -- Modul - varchar(50)
										@LetrehozoEmail,        -- Recipients - varchar(260)
										NULL,        -- CopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
										NULL,        -- BlindCopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
										@Targy,        -- Subject - varchar(200)
										@Szoveg,        -- Body - varchar(max)
										'HTML',        -- BodyFormat - varchar(20)
										'Normal',        -- Importance - varchar(100)
										'',        -- FileAttachments - varchar(8000)
										0,         -- MailItemID - int
										GETDATE(), -- Created - datetime
										0,      -- Success - bit
										0,         -- Deleted - tinyint
										@TemplateID,         -- EmailTemplateID - int
										@LetrehozoID,         -- CreatedBy - int
										@CimzettID,         -- SentToJelentkezoID - int
										0          -- SentToJelentkezoTablaID - tinyint
										)

									SET @MailSendLogID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

									EXEC [dbo].[msk_SendMail_dll] 	
											@Modul = 'TOB',
											@Recipients = @LetrehozoEmail,
											@CopyRecipients  = '',
											@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
											@Subject = @Targy,
											@Body = @Szoveg,
											@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
											@Importance = 'Normal',
											@FileAttachments = NULL,
											@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
											@CreatedBy = @LetrehozoID,
											@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
											@CimzettTablaID = 0,
											@MailSendLogID = @MailSendLogID

									--exec [dbo].[msk_SendMail]
									--	@Modul = 'TOB',
									--	@Recipients = @LetrehozoEmail,
									--	@CopyRecipients  = NULL,
									--	@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
									--	@Subject = @Targy,
									--	@Body = @Szoveg,
									--	@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
									--	@Importance = 'Normal',
									--	@FileAttachments = NULL,
									--	@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
									--	@CreatedBy = @CimzettID,
									--	@CimzettID = @LetrehozoID,
									--	@CimzettTablaID = 0
								END

								FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor
								INTO @ID, @StatuszOLD, @StatuszNEW
							END; 

							CLOSE @MyCursor;
							DEALLOCATE @MYCursor;
						END;
        ]]>			</RunSQL>
		</BeforeSave>
		<AfterSave>
			<RunSQL>
				<![CDATA[
                UPDATE msk_tob_allashirdetesek SET Toborzo_info = '[##Field.Toborzonev##]' + ' ' + '[##Field.Toborzotelefonszam##]' WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = '[##Field.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID##]'

                -- emailt küldés
                  EXEC dbo.msk_tob_AdHoc_email_kuldes '[##Field.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID##]', 'false', '[##Session.UserID##]'
            	]]>
			</RunSQL>
		</AfterSave>
	</Methods>
</BusinessObject>

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\BusinessObject\BusinessObjectMSKTOBKeptar.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<BusinessObject xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/businessobject">
  <DataTable>msk_tob_keptar</DataTable>
  <UniqueIDColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</UniqueIDColumn>
  <Fields>
    <Field name="Msk_tob_keptarID" />
    <Field name="DocumentID" isDocument="true" />
    <Field name="CompanyID" />
    <Field name="Kulcsszavak" />
  </Fields>
  <Methods>
    <OnValidate type="SQL" return="string" default=""><![CDATA[
        IF EXISTS (SELECT * FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE StatuszID IN (20,21,22,23,25) AND FenykepURL = (SELECT RenamedFilename FROM dbo.Document WHERE DocumentID='[##Field.DocumentID##]'))
	        SELECT 'A kép használatban van egy aktív álláshirdetésen, ezért nem törölhető!'
        ELSE
	        SELECT ''
      ]]></OnValidate>
    <AfterSave>
      <Module className="HOP_TOB_Keptar.Keptar" action="mentes">[##LocalProgramPath##]\HOP_TOB_Keptar.dll</Module>
    </AfterSave>
    <AfterDelete>
      <Module className="HOP_TOB_Keptar.Keptar" action="torles">[##LocalProgramPath##]\HOP_TOB_Keptar.dll</Module>
    </AfterDelete>
  </Methods>
</BusinessObject>

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\BusinessObject\BusinessObjectMSKTOBKeresesiKerelem.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<BusinessObject xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/businessobject">
  <DataTable>msk_tob_keresesikerelem</DataTable>
  <UniqueIDColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID</UniqueIDColumn>
  <Fields>
    <Field name="Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID" />
    <Field name="Cim" requestValidatorCharacterGroup="Anything" />
    <Field name="StatuszID" />
    <Field name="Iktatoszam" />
    <Field name="Engedelyezesidatum" />
    <Field name="Munkakor" />
    <Field name="Lejaratidatum" />
    <Field name="Pozicioszam" />
    <Field name="TeruletiigazgatosagID" />
    <Field name="SzakteruletID" />
    <Field name="SzervezetiegyesegID" />
    <Field name="SzerzodesfajtaID" />
    <Field name="MunkavegzeshelyeID" />
    <Field name="Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb" />
    <Field name="Cv" />
    <Field name="MunkakorcsoportID" />
    <Field name="FoglalkoztatasifokID" />
    <Field name="Kepzes_fajtaID" />
    <Field name="Kepzes_szakiranyID" />
    <Field name="MMKkod" />
    <Field name="Berlatszik" />
    <Field name="Berkotelezo" />
    <Field name="Map_job" />
    <Field name="Idtoborzo1" />
    <Field name="Idtoborzo2" />
    <Field name="Idengedelyezo" />
    <Field name="Idceg" />
    <Field name="Szerzodes_befejezes" />
    <Field name="Lezaras" />
  </Fields>
  <Methods>
    <OnValidate type="SQL" return="string" default=""><![CDATA[
			/*valami*/
		    IF '[##Field.Lezaras##]' = 'true' AND
			    EXISTS (SELECT * FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Idkeresesikerelem='[##Field.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID##]' AND StatuszID NOT IN (20,24) AND Deleted=0) 
            SELECT 'A keresési kérlem csak abban az esetben zárható le, amennyiben keresési kérelemhez nem tartozik álláshirdetés, vagy az álláshirdetés Lezárt vagy Terv státuszban van.'
            ]]>
    </OnValidate>

					declare @cnt int = (select count(*) from dbo.msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and Idkeresesikerelem = '[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')
						update msk_tob_keresesikerelem set Pozicioszam = @cnt where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = '[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]'
						update msk_kex_allasajanlatok set poziciok_szama=@cnt where msk_kex_allasajanlatokID in (select Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID from msk_tob_allashirdetesek where Idkeresesikerelem='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]') 
					
				
						
				]]>				
			</RunSQL>

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\BusinessObject\BusinessObjectMSKTOBPozicioEdit.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<BusinessObject xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/businessobject">
	<DataTable>msk_tob_pozicio</DataTable>
	<UniqueIDColumn>PozicioID</UniqueIDColumn>
	<Fields>
		<Field name="PozicioID" />
		<Field name="Engedelyezesidatum" />
		<Field name="StatuszID" />
		<Field name="TorlesindokID" />
		<Field name="PozicioInfo"/>
		<Field name="PozicioVisszavDatum"/>
		<Field name="Pre_Torles"/>
	</Fields>
	<Methods>
		<AfterLoad>
			<RunSQL>
				<![CDATA[ update msk_tob_pozicio set Pre_Torles = NULL where PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]' ]]></RunSQL>
		</AfterLoad>
		<AfterSave>
			<RunSQL>
				<![CDATA[

					IF '[##Field.ClickedButton##]'='Save' begin

							if (select ISNULL(Pre_Torles,0) from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]') IN (1) 
							begin
								--valójában törlés és indoklása és nem Save
								update msk_tob_pozicio set deleted=1,Pre_Torles=NULL WHERE PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]'
								
								declare @cnt int = (select count(*) from dbo.msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and Idkeresesikerelem = '[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')
								update msk_tob_keresesikerelem set Pozicioszam = @cnt where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = '[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]'
								update msk_kex_allasajanlatok set poziciok_szama=@cnt where msk_kex_allasajanlatokID in (select Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID from msk_tob_allashirdetesek where Idkeresesikerelem='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]') 
								
							end
							else begin
								--valós Save
								
								if (SELECT top 1 poziciotipus FROM msk_tob_headpozicio
										WHERE Idkeresesikerelem ='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]' AND DELETED<2 ) = 41 begin
									--tanfolyamos esetben:
									update msk_tob_headpozicio set Engedelyezesidatum='[##Field.Engedelyezesidatum##]' WHERE Idkeresesikerelem ='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]' AND DELETED<2
									update msk_tob_pozicio set Engedelyezesidatum='[##Field.Engedelyezesidatum##]' WHERE Idkeresesikerelem ='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]' AND DELETED<2
										
								end
							end
					end
					
					IF '[##Field.ClickedButton##]'='Delete' begin
						update dbo.msk_tob_pozicio SET Pre_Torles=1 WHERE PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]'
					end

				]]>
			</RunSQL>
		</AfterSave>
	</Methods>

</BusinessObject>

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\ComboDefinition\ComboMSKKEXToborzo.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<ComboDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/combodefinition">
  <SourceType>Database</SourceType>
  <Source>
    <Database>
      <SelectionString><![CDATA[
        IF '[##Session.UserID##]' IN (SELECT DISTINCT p.PeopleID
        FROM People as p LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople as pgp ON p.PeopleID=pgp.PeopleID left JOIN People as pp ON pgp.GroupID=pp.PeopleID
        WHERE pp.TechnicalName='Group_ITA'
        AND p.Deleted=0 AND pgp.Deleted=0 AND pp.Deleted=0)
        BEGIN
          SELECT DISTINCT
          p.PeopleID, p.Name
          FROM People as p LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople as pgp ON p.PeopleID=pgp.PeopleID left JOIN People as pp ON pgp.GroupID=pp.PeopleID
          WHERE
          pp.TechnicalName='Group_KEXTOB' AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
          AND p.Deleted=0 AND pgp.Deleted=0 AND pp.Deleted=0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true' AND 1=1 ORDER BY p.Name
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
          SELECT DISTINCT
          p.PeopleID, p.Name
          FROM People as p LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople as pgp ON p.PeopleID=pgp.PeopleID left JOIN People as pp ON pgp.GroupID=pp.PeopleID
          WHERE
          pp.TechnicalName='Group_KEXTOB' AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
          AND p.Deleted=0 AND pgp.Deleted=0 AND pp.Deleted=0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true' AND p.BUKRS=(SELECT BUKRS FROM People Where PeopleID = '[##Session.UserID##]') AND 1=1 ORDER BY p.Name
        END
				]]></SelectionString>
      <KeyColumn>PeopleID</KeyColumn>
      <ValueColumn>Name</ValueColumn>
    </Database>
  </Source>
</ComboDefinition>

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\ComboDefinition\ComboMSKTOBEngedelyezoPSearch.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<ComboDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/combodefinition">
  <SourceType>Database</SourceType>
  <Source>
    <Database>
      <SelectionString><![CDATA[
        IF '[##Session.UserID##]' IN (SELECT DISTINCT p.PeopleID
        FROM People as p LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople as pgp ON p.PeopleID=pgp.PeopleID left JOIN People as pp ON pgp.GroupID=pp.PeopleID
        WHERE pp.TechnicalName='Group_ITA' and pgp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted=0 and pp.deleted=0)
        BEGIN
          SELECT DISTINCT
                  Idengedelyezo as Idengedelyezo, p.Name as Nev
                  FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk LEFT JOIN dbo.People p ON p.PeopleID=kk.Idengedelyezo
                  WHERE
                  kk.Deleted=0 AND p.Deleted=0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
                  AND 1=1
                  ORDER BY p.Name
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
          SELECT DISTINCT
                  Idengedelyezo as Idengedelyezo, p.Name as Nev
                  FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk LEFT JOIN dbo.People p ON p.PeopleID=kk.Idengedelyezo
                  WHERE
                  kk.Deleted=0 AND p.Deleted=0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
                  AND p.BUKRS=(SELECT BUKRS FROM People Where PeopleID = '[##Session.UserID##]')
                  AND 1=1
                  ORDER BY p.Name
        END]]></SelectionString>
      <KeyColumn>Idengedelyezo</KeyColumn>
      <ValueColumn>Nev</ValueColumn>
    </Database>
  </Source>
</ComboDefinition>

        IF '[##Session.UserID##]' IN (SELECT DISTINCT p.PeopleID
        FROM People as p LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople as pgp ON p.PeopleID=pgp.PeopleID left JOIN People as pp ON pgp.GroupID=pp.PeopleID
        WHERE pp.TechnicalName='Group_ITA' AND pgp.Deleted=0 AND pp.Deleted=0)
        BEGIN
          SELECT DISTINCT
                  sz.Kod as Kod, sz.Nev as Nev
                  FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_szervezetiegyseg sz ON sz.Kod=kk.SzervezetiegyesegID
                  WHERE kk.Deleted=0

        END

                  sz.Kod as Kod, sz.Nev as Nev
                  FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_szervezetiegyseg sz ON sz.Kod=kk.SzervezetiegyesegID
                  WHERE kk.Deleted=0
                  AND sz.BUKRS = (SELECT TOP 1 BUKRS FROM People Where PeopleID = '[##Session.UserID##]')
				          AND 1=1 ORDER BY sz.Nev
        END
       ]]></SelectionString>

            WHERE
            (pp.TechnicalName='Group_KEXTOB')
            AND p.Deleted=0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
            AND p.BUKRS=(SELECT BUKRS FROM People Where PeopleID = '[##Session.UserID##]')
            AND 1=1 ORDER BY p.Name

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\XML\DataDefinition\DataDefinitionMSKTOBAllashirdetesek.xml =====

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<DataDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/datadefinition">
  <SqlSelect>
    FROM msk_tob_allashirdetesek h
    left join msk_tob_LookupList s on s.LookupListID = h.StatuszID
    left join msk_tob_keresesikerelem m on m.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=h.Idkeresesikerelem
    left join msk_tob_telepulesek t on t.Msk_tob_telepulesekID = m.MunkavegzeshelyeID
    WHERE h.Deleted=0 AND 1=1
  </SqlSelect>
  <Columns>
    <Column name="Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID">
      <Definition>[Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>h.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>

        (CASE 
            when h.StatuszID=20 then 'terv'
          WHEN h.StatuszID=21 THEN 'engedelyezett'
          WHEN h.StatuszID=22 THEN 'publikalt'
          WHEN h.StatuszID=23 THEN 'lejart'
          WHEN h.StatuszID=24 THEN 'lezart'
          WHEN h.StatuszID=25 THEN 'elküldott'

        END) as szin
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Publikalas">
      <Definition>
				<![CDATA[
            (Case when (h.StatuszID=21)
			
			    and ( select count(*) from msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and Idkeresesikerelem=m.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID)>0
			
			    and (m.Idengedelyezo = '[##Session.UserID##]' 
                OR '[##Session.UserID##]' IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)) 
					AND ISNULL((SELECT CodeValue FROM dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup WHERE Code='CsoportosAllasPulikalas' AND Deleted=0),'false')='false'
            THEN '<div class="msk_button_public" style="left:160px;top:110px;"><b><span class="efi-plus-circled" style="font-size:20px;"></span>Publikálás</b></div>' ELSE '' END) as Publikalas
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Screen_terv">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
        (CASE 
          When (h.StatuszID=20) then Targy
          WHEN h.StatuszID=21 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=22 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=23 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=24 THEN ''
          WHEN (h.StatuszID=25) THEN Targy
        END) as Screen_terv
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Screen_eng">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
        (CASE 
          --When ( (not(m.Lezaras=0 or m.Lezaras is null)) or m.Lejaratidatum<=getdate()) then Targy
          When h.StatuszID=20 then ''
          WHEN (h.StatuszID=21) THEN Targy
          WHEN h.StatuszID=22 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=23 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=24 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=25 THEN ''
        END) as Screen_eng
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Screen_publikalt">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
        (CASE 
          When h.StatuszID=20 then ''
          WHEN (h.StatuszID=21) THEN ''
          WHEN (h.StatuszID=22) THEN Targy
          WHEN h.StatuszID=23 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=24 THEN ''
          WHEN h.StatuszID=25 THEN ''
        END) as Screen_publikalt
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID</IdColumn>

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<DataDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/datadefinition">
  <SqlSelect distinct="true"><![CDATA[
        FROM People p
        LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
        LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
        WHERE
        pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_TOBENG'
        AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0  AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true'
        AND 1=1
    ]]></SqlSelect>
  <Columns>
    <Column name="PeopleID">
      <Definition>p.[PeopleID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>PeopleID</IdColumn>
      <OutFilter>
        <Alias>PeopleID_ID</Alias>
        <Type>Out</Type>
      </OutFilter>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Name">
      <Definition>p.[Name]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>PeopleID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="PERNR">
      <Definition>p.[PERNR]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>PeopleID</IdColumn>
    </Column>

<DataDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/datadefinition">
  <SqlSelect>FROM msk_tob_keptar k LEFT JOIN Document d ON d.DocumentID=k.DocumentID WHERE k.deleted=0 AND 1=1</SqlSelect>
  <Columns>
    <Column name="Msk_tob_keptarID">
      <Definition>k.[Msk_tob_keptarID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</IdColumn>
      <OutFilter>
        <Alias>Msk_tob_keptarID_ID</Alias>
        <Type>Out</Type>
      </OutFilter>
    </Column>
    <Column name="DocumentID">
      <Definition>k.[DocumentID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="DocumentIDFileInterfaceID">
      <Definition><![CDATA[CAST(k.DocumentID  AS VARCHAR(20)) as DocumentIDFileInterfaceID]]></Definition>
      <OutFilter>
        <Alias>DocumentIDFileInterfaceID</Alias>
        <Type>Param</Type>
      </OutFilter>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</IdColumn>
      <UseFileInterface>true</UseFileInterface>
    </Column>
    <Column name="CompanyID">
      <Definition>k.[CompanyID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Kulcsszavak">
      <Definition>k.[Kulcsszavak]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keptarID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="FileType">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
          (CASE WHEN (SUBSTRING(d.[OriginalFileName], LEN(d.[OriginalFileName]) - (CHARINDEX('.', REVERSE(d.[OriginalFileName]))- 2 ), 8000)) IN ('bmp', 'cvs', 'doc', 'docx', 'html', 'iso', 'jpg', 'msg', 'odt', 'pdf', 'png', 'ppt', 'sql', 'txt', 'zip')
				    THEN SUBSTRING(d.OriginalFileName, LEN(d.OriginalFileName)-(CHARINDEX('.', REVERSE(d.OriginalFileName))-2), 8000)
			      ELSE 'other'
			    END) AS FileType 
        ]]></Definition>
    </Column>
    <Column name="CardTitle">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
          SUBSTRING(d.[OriginalFilename], 0,(LEN(d.[OriginalFilename]) + 1 - CHARINDEX('.', REVERSE(d.[OriginalFilename])))) AS CardTitle
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>DocumentID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
  </Columns>
  <InFilters>
    <InFilter>
      <Alias>Msk_tob_keptarID_ID</Alias>
      <ConnectedColumnDefinition>k.[Msk_tob_keptarID]</ConnectedColumnDefinition>
    </InFilter>
  </InFilters>
</DataDefinition>

                    ELSE ''                    
                    END) as Kartya_statusz

          When k.Lezaras=0 and (ISNULL(k.Idtoborzo2,0) = '[##Session.UserID##]') and (ISNULL(k.Idtoborzo1,0) <> '[##Session.UserID##]') and (ISNULL(k.Idengedelyezo,0) <> '[##Session.UserID##]')
          and '[##Session.UserID##]' NOT IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
												LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
												LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
											WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
													AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)
          then k.Cim
          ELSE ''
        END) as Screen_megtekint
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Screen_alap">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
        (CASE 
          When k.Lezaras=0 and ('[##Session.UserID##]' IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
                      AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)
                      OR '[##Session.UserID##]' = k.Idtoborzo1 
                      OR '[##Session.UserID##]' = k.Idengedelyezo) then k.Cim
          ELSE ''
        END) as Screen_alap
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Screen_lezart">
      <Definition><![CDATA[
        (CASE 
          When k.Lezaras=1 then k.Cim
          else ''
        END) as Screen_lezart
        ]]></Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
  </Columns>

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<DataDefinition xmlns="http://effector.hu/schema/ns/datadefinition">
  <SqlSelect>
    FROM Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok as v
    LEFT JOIN  People AS p ON v.Idvezeto = p.PeopleID
    LEFT JOIN msk_kex_LookupList as ls ON v.mjgy = ls.LookupListID
    LEFT JOIN msk_kex_LookupList as ll ON v.Statuszolovezeto+11 = ll.LookupListID
    WHERE v.Deleted=0 AND 1=1
  </SqlSelect>
  <Columns>
    <Column name="Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID">
      <Definition>v.[Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID</IdColumn>

      </OutFilter>

    </Column>
    <Column name="Idkeresesikerelem">
      <Definition>v.[Idkeresesikerelem]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID</IdColumn>
    </Column>

    </Column>
    <Column name="statusz_LookupValue">
      <Definition>ls.[LookupValue] as statusz_LookupValue</Definition>
      <IdColumn>msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetokID</IdColumn>
    </Column>
    <Column name="Statuszolovezeto">
      <Definition>v.[Statuszolovezeto]</Definition>
      <IdColumn>msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetokID</IdColumn>
    </Column>

      <IdColumn>msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetokID</IdColumn>

		</Column>

		</Column>

			<Visible>true</Visible>
		</Column>

			<Visible>true</Visible>
		</Column>

			<Summary column="Iktatoszam" type="Custom">Pozíció szám:</Summary>
			<Summary column="Engedelyezesidatum" type="Count"/>
		</Summaries>
	</TableViewOptions>
	<OutFilterColumn>PozicioID</OutFilterColumn>

			<Control>
				<Name>Filter_ID</Name>
				<Type>TextSearch</Type>
				<Caption>ID</Caption>
				<ConnectedColumnDefinition>PozicioID</ConnectedColumnDefinition>
				<Operator>=</Operator>
				<Width>200</Width>
				<DefaultValue type="Constant" return="int" default="">'[##Filter.PozicioID_ID##]'</DefaultValue>
				<Visible>false</Visible>
			</Control>
			<!--IDFILTER-->
			<Control>
				<Name>NewObject</Name>
				<Type>NewObjectButton</Type>
				<Caption>Új pozíció hozzáadása</Caption>
				<BusinessObject>BusinessObjectMSKTOBMsktobpoziciopoz</BusinessObject>
				<Screen>ScreenMSKTOBPozicio</Screen>
				<Visible type="SQL" default="true" return="boolean">
					<![CDATA[
			  if isnull('[##Filter.msk_kex_allasajanlatokID_ID##]','')<>'' or '[##Special.ScreenName##]' <> 'ScreenMSKTOBKeresesiKerelemEdit'
				or (select isnull(idceg,0) from msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')=0
				or (select Lezaras from msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')=1
				select 'false'
			  ]]>
				</Visible>
			</Control>
			<Control>
				<Name>FilterDEL</Name>
				<Type>BoolSearch</Type>
				<Caption>Törölt pozíciók</Caption>
				<ConnectedColumnDefinition><![CDATA[(case when p.[Deleted]=1 then 'true' else 'false' end)]]></ConnectedColumnDefinition>
				<Operator>=</Operator>
				<DefaultValue>false</DefaultValue>
				<IsIndeterminateAllowed>false</IsIndeterminateAllowed>
			</Control>

				<Visible type="SQL" return="boolean" default="false">
		 select case when Automata is not null then 1 else 0 end from msk_tob_headpozicio where Idkeresesikerelem='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]'
				</Visible>
			</Control>
			<!--DELFILTER-->
		</Controls>

        <Caption>mjgy:</Caption>
        <ConnectedColumnDefinition>[PSTLZ]</ConnectedColumnDefinition>
        <DefaultValue type="Constant" return="int" default="">[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]</DefaultValue>
        <Query>
          (
          SELECT P.PERNR
          FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok] AS V
          LEFT JOIN (SELECT * FROM People WHERE Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(PeopleID)='true') as P ON V.Idvezeto = P.PeopleID
          WHERE V.idkeresesikerelem = #param# AND V.Mjgy = 10 AND V.Deleted= 0
          )
        </Query>
        <Operator>in</Operator>
        <Visible>false</Visible>
      </Control>
      <!--Kivéve a már kiválasztott dolgozók-->
      <Control>
        <Name>Filter_vanmar</Name>
        <Type>TextSearch</Type>
        <Caption>Van már:</Caption>
        <ConnectedColumnDefinition> NOT [PeopleID]</ConnectedColumnDefinition>
        <DefaultValue type="Constant" return="int" default="">[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]</DefaultValue>
        <Query>
          (
          SELECT V.IDvezeto
          FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok] AS V
          WHERE V.idkeresesikerelem = #param# AND V.Mjgy = 9 AND V.Deleted= 0
          )
        </Query>
        <Operator>in</Operator>
        <Visible>false</Visible>
      </Control>
      <!--TODO:Befejezni a vezetői szerepkör figyelembevételével-->
      <!--
      <Control>
        <Name>Filter_Munkaltato</Name>  
        <Type>TextSearch</Type>
        <Caption>Munkáltató:</Caption>
        <ConnectedColumnDefinition>[PSTLZ]</ConnectedColumnDefinition>
        <DefaultValue type="SQL" return="int" default="">SELECT PERNR FROM People WHERE PeopleID = [##Filter.idmunkaltato_ID##]</DefaultValue>
        <Operator>%like%</Operator>
        <Visible type="Constant" return="boolean">false</Visible>
      </Control>

    </Controls>
  </ControlPanel>
</DisplayDefinition>

				    if (('[##Field.Hatarbe##]' == 'True') || ('[##Field.Hatarki##]' == 'True'))

					    function dt(dat){
                            d = dat.split(" ");
                            date = d[0].split("-");
                            time = d[1].split(":");    
                            res = new Date(parseInt(date[0],10),parseInt(date[1],10)-1,parseInt(date[2],10),parseInt(time[0],10),parseInt(time[1],10))    
                            if (isNaN(res)) res=''; else res=res.getTime();
                            return res;
                        }
                        var f = dt("[##Field.Oda##]");
                        var t = dt("[##Field.Vissza##]");
                        var e = dt("[##Field.Datumhatar##]");

                        if (f!='' || t!='' ) {
                            if ( e >= f && e <= t) 
							{
                                "";
                            } 
							else 
							{
							    "A határátlépés időpontjának az adott jármű utazási időpontjai között kell lennie!";
							}
                        }
						
					} 
					else 
					{
					    "";  //"[##Field.Hatarbe##]";
					}
			        ]]></ValidateRule>

              SELECT 'true'
            ELSE
              SELECT 'false'
          ]]>
			</Visible>
			<Required type="SQL" return="boolean" default="false">
				<![CDATA[
            IF (select ISNULL(Pre_Torles,0) from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]') IN (1)
              SELECT 'true'
            ELSE
              SELECT 'false'
          ]]>
			</Required>
			<Readonly type="SQL" return="boolean" default="false">
				<![CDATA[
			if '[##Field.Deleted##]'='1' begin
				select 'true'
			end else begin				
				if (select ISNULL(TorlesindokID,'') from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]') = '' 
				  SELECT 'false'
				ELSE
				  SELECT 'true'
			end
          ]]>
			</Readonly>
		</Rules>
	</ControlGroup>


	        <ControlGroup name="ClickedButton">
                <Controls>
                    <Control>
                        <Type>TextBox</Type>
                        <Name>CheckBox_ClickedButton</Name>
                        <BindingName>ClickedButton</BindingName>
                        <ComputedValue type="SQL" return="string" default="">select '[##Special.ClickedButton##]'</ComputedValue>
                    </Control>
                </Controls>
                <Rules>
                    <Visible>false</Visible>
                </Rules>
            </ControlGroup>	

            <ControlGroup name="ButtonGroup">
            <Controls>
              <Control>
                <Type>SaveButton</Type>
                <Name>Save</Name>				
                <Caption>[#EditFormPanel.SaveButton#]</Caption>
				  <Visible default="false" return="boolean" type="SQL">
					  <![CDATA[
			if '[##Field.Deleted##]'='1'
          or (select Lezaras from msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')=1
			begin
				select 'false'
			end else begin					  					  
				if [dbo].[msk_tob_fn_menu_lathatosag] ('ToborzasiFolyg','[##Session.UserID##]',0)=1 begin
						select 'true'
				end else begin

					if [dbo].[msk_tob_fn_menu_lathatosag] ('Toborzo','[##Session.UserID##]',0)=1 begin
						if '[##Filter.StatuszID_ID##]' in (32) begin
							select 'true'
						end
					end
				
				end
			end
            ]]>
				  </Visible>
              </Control>
              <Control>
                <Type>CancelButton</Type>
                <Name>Cancel</Name>
                <Caption>[#EditFormPanel.CancelButton#]</Caption>
                <Width>50</Width>
              </Control>
              <Control>
                <Type>SaveButton</Type>
                <Name>Delete</Name>
				<ButtonLooksLike>DeleteButton</ButtonLooksLike>
				<CloseWindow>false</CloseWindow>
                <Caption>[#EditFormPanel.DeleteButton#]</Caption>
                <Width>50</Width>
				  <Visible default="false" return="boolean" type="SQL">
					  <![CDATA[
if '[##Field.Deleted##]'='1' 
	or isnull('[##Filter.msk_kex_allasajanlatokID_ID##]','')<>'' 
	or (select Lezaras from msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID='[##Filter.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID##]')=1
begin
	select 'false'
end else begin					  					  


		if '[##Filter.JumpType##]' <> 'New' begin
					  
			if (select ISNULL(Pre_Torles,0) from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID='[##Field.PozicioID##]') NOT IN (1) begin
					  
				if [dbo].[msk_tob_fn_menu_lathatosag] ('ToborzasiFolyg','[##Session.UserID##]',0)=1 
					and '[##Filter.StatuszID_ID##]' in ('32')
				begin
					select 'true'
				end 
			
			end
			
	    end

end

]]>
				  </Visible>
				  
		
              </Control>
            </Controls>
          </ControlGroup>      
            </ControlGroups>
